---
layout: lexeme
lexeme: Sulattaja

###  Sulattaja₁

* _This rare proper noun overlaps more common *Sulattaja* (melter)_
* UPOS:  PROPN
* in KOTUS dictionary under:  10
* Origins: finer 
* Possible NER class:  GEO
* Blacklisted:  PROPN-BLOCKING
